Based completely in the source code found in:

  - [https://github.com/alps-chalmers/agda101](https://github.com/alps-chalmers/agda101)

I just made minor changes for self-understanding. I don't claim authority of any class.

Data type for a code segment. Can be a regular segment, block of code
segments, a par statement (cobegin/coend) as well as while loops and if
statements.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="2881" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="Seg"></a><a id="2886" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#2886" class="Datatype">Seg</a> <a id="2890" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2892" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="2896" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="LTL._==n_"></a><a id="4550" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4550" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_==n_</a>        <a id="4563" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4565" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4566" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4566" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="4568" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4570" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#1023" class="Datatype">NVar</a><a id="4574" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4576" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4578" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4579" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4579" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="4581" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4583" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#97" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="4584" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4586" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4588" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#3976" class="Datatype">LTL</a>     <a id="4596" class="Comment">-- Nat variable x has the value n</a>
  <a id="LTL._==b_"></a><a id="4632" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4632" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_==b_</a>        <a id="4645" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4647" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4648" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4648" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="4650" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4652" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#1123" class="Datatype">BVar</a><a id="4656" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4658" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4660" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4661" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4661" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="4663" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4665" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#1123" class="Datatype">BVar</a><a id="4669" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4671" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4673" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#3976" class="Datatype">LTL</a>  <a id="4678" class="Comment">-- Bool variable x has the value of y</a>
  <a id="LTL.isTrue"></a><a id="4718" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4718" class="InductiveConstructor">isTrue</a>       <a id="4731" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4733" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4734" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#4734" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="4736" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4738" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#1123" class="Datatype">BVar</a><a id="4742" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4744" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4746" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#3976" class="Datatype">LTL</a>               <a id="4764" class="Comment">-- Variable x has the value -- true</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## The LTL-rule data type

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="6687" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="LTLRule"></a><a id="6692" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#6692" class="Datatype">LTLRule</a> <a id="6700" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6702" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="6706" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="LTLRule.∧-e₁"></a><a id="6714" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#6714" class="InductiveConstructor">∧-e₁</a>   <a id="6721" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6723" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#3976" class="Datatype">LTL</a> <a id="6727" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6729" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#6692" class="Datatype">LTLRule</a>        <a id="6744" class="Comment">-- and-elimination on first element</a>
  <a id="LTLRule.∧-e₂"></a><a id="6782" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#6782" class="InductiveConstructor">∧-e₂</a>   <a id="6789" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6791" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#3976" class="Datatype">LTL</a> <a id="6795" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6797" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#6692" class="Datatype">LTLRule</a>        <a id="6812" class="Comment">-- and-elimination on second element</a>

## Propositional logic representation

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="10363" class="Comment">-- Representation of propositional logic</a>
<a id="10404" class="Comment">-- data Props : Set where</a>
<a id="10430" class="Comment">--   T ⊥         : Props</a>
<a id="10455" class="Comment">--   _∧_ _∨_ _⇒_ : Props → Props → Props</a>
<a id="10496" class="Comment">--   p&#39;          : ℕ → Props</a>
<a id="10525" class="Comment">--   ~_          : Props → Props</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Translator

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="10598" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Translator"></a><a id="10605" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#10605" class="Module">Translator</a> <a id="10616" class="Keyword">where</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Translator for concurrent programs. Translates program representations into
transition relations (TransRel). The relations keep track of the LTL-formulas
related to the program statements of the programs.

### Actions

Data type for actions, reference to what happened when translating the program

### Hoare-style Triples

Represents transition relations, < pre > action < post >, where pre is the
precondition of the program statement, action the reference to the type of
program statement, and post the postcondition of the statement.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="11974" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="TransRel"></a><a id="11979" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#11979" class="Datatype">TransRel</a> <a id="11988" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11990" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="11994" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="TransRel.&lt;_&gt;_&lt;_&gt;"></a><a id="12002" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#12002" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">&lt;_&gt;_&lt;_&gt;</a> <a id="12010" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12012" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12013" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#12013" class="Bound">c₁</a> <a id="12016" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12018" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#3976" class="Datatype">LTL</a><a id="12021" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12023" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12025" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#10950" class="Datatype">Action</a> <a id="12032" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12034" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12035" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#12035" class="Bound">c₂</a> <a id="12038" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12040" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#3976" class="Datatype">LTL</a><a id="12043" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12045" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12047" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#11979" class="Datatype">TransRel</a>  <a id="12057" class="Comment">-- Hoare-style Triple</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


Translates a program statement into the corresponding `TransRel`.
  * `l`: Program label of the program statement.
  * `Stm`: The program statement.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="transStm"></a><a id="12255" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#12255" class="Function">transStm</a> <a id="12264" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12266" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#906" class="Datatype">Label</a> <a id="12272" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12274" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#2406" class="Datatype">Stm</a> <a id="12278" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12280" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#11979" class="Datatype">TransRel</a>

Flattens a list of lists into a single list.

Converts a list of segments and a label, representing a single block segment,
into a list of `TransRel`. The result contains the representation of the program
flow.

* `p`: Label of the parent segment.
* `List Seg`: List of all child segments.

Converts a list of segments into a single `LTL`. The list represents all child
segments initiated by a parent `par` segment. The result is an `LTL` used as a
precondition in order to allow the parent segment to be considered executed.

Helper function for translate that uses different translation approaches
depending on the type of segment to be translated.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="15187" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="15191" class="Keyword">TERMINATING</a> <a id="15203" class="Symbol">#-}</a> <a id="15207" class="Comment">-- used to guarantee that there is no infinite looping</a>

  <a id="16676" class="Comment">-- Translate the if statement</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


Translate function that takes a program and returns a list of TransRel.
The list consists of two parts, first the statement specific translations,
the second the program flow relations between the segments.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="translate"></a><a id="16940" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#16940" class="Function">translate</a> <a id="16950" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16952" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#3744" class="Record">Prog</a> <a id="16957" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="16959" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.List.html#80" class="Datatype">List</a> <a id="16964" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#11979" class="Datatype">TransRel</a>

## Rules to construct proofs

Contains rules to use when construction proofs. Also has functions to check if
rules are used legally. Used in ProofChecker

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="17229" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Rules"></a><a id="17236" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-10-23-hoare-triples.md %}{% raw %}#17236" class="Module">Rules</a> <a id="17242" class="Keyword">where</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Data type for program rules, indexed with rule and `LTL`. Specifically for
proof-steps regarding the programs

                                             <a id="18133" class="Comment">-- control progression</a>
